Everyone who worked at the hotel was very friendly. The people who welcomed us, the ones who helped us check in quickly, and the people who cleaned our room made us feel very special. They were all very kind and paid attention to the little things, which made our stay very nice.

We really enjoyed the food from room service too. There were many tasty choices that were more delicious than we expected. Eating these meals made our time at the hotel even better.

Our room was high up and had an amazing view of Chongqing. This made our stay even more special. We chose a room for smokers, but the air in our room was still fresh because the air system worked really well.

The hotel was in a great place for getting around the city. There was a metro station close by which was very handy. For those visiting, we suggest using Didi for getting around because it's cheap and taxis find it easy to get to the hotel.

The hotel looked really nice too, including the lobby and all the areas we saw. Breakfast was incredible, with lots of different foods from both Western and Eastern styles. It was great to have so many choices. Also, it was helpful that some of the hotel staff could speak English, which we didn't find everywhere. They even had robots helping out, which was really cool and modern.

This hotel in Chongqing had lots of great points like excellent service and cleanliness. It's a really good choice in Chongqing for anyone looking for a place that offers a good deal, great service, cleanliness, and a convenient location. We're very thankful to everyone there for making our visit a good one, and we would happily stay there again.
